Construction of weigths

Survey Variables
================

-   Randomization orders: A2:3, B2, C1, D1:3, E1, E3, F1:2, E2:4, I8,
-   Timers: D1-D3

### Block B: Performance Politics in the Media

### Block C: Issue Association

<table class=" lightable-classic-2 table" style='font-size: 13px; font-family: "Arial Narrow", "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; width: auto !important; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;'>

partijleider\]?

<table class=" lightable-classic-2 table" style='font-size: 13px; font-family: "Arial Narrow", "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; width: auto !important; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;'>

trust\_statements

</td>

</td>

</td>

</td>

</td>

7
</td>

I feel well represented by Dutch politicians.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">

</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
8
</td>

What in politics is called ‘making compromises’ is actually just
betraying your principles.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Wat men in de politiek ‘het sluiten van compromissen’ noemt, is
eigenlijk gewoon het verraden van je principes.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
9
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
A strong head of government is good for the Netherlands, even if he
stretches the rules a bit to get things done.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Een sterke regeringsleider is goed voor Nederland, ook als deze de
regels wat oprekt om dingen voor elkaar te krijgen.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">

not by politicians.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
De belangrijkste politieke beslissingen moeten worden genomen door het
volk en niet door politici.
</td>

Label
</td>

gov\_termination

Question wording ENG
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 65em; ">
Some said the government should resign, for example, because of the
benefits affair. Others said that the government should stay on, for
example, because without a government there is no support for coronation
measures. What do you think?
</td>
</tr>

Question wording NL
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 65em; ">

toeslagenaffaire. Anderen zeiden dat de regering moest aanblijven,
bijvoorbeeld omdat zonder regering er geen draagvlak is voor
coronamaatregelen. Wat vindt u?
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>

</td>

leader\_selection
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 15em; ">
Question wording ENG
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 65em; ">
You will now be shown 3 statements that have to do with Dutch party
leaders. We would like to know from you to what extent the statement
applies to the party leader. Below you can indicate whether a party
leader is unknown to you.
</td>
</tr>

Question wording NL
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 65em; ">
U krijgt nu 3 stellingen te zien die te maken hebben met de Nederlandse
partijleiders. Wij willen graag van u weten in hoeverre de uitspraak van
toepassing is op de partijleider. Hieronder kunt u aangeven of een
partijleider onbekend is bij u.
</td>

Label

corona\_policy

We would like to ask you for your opinion on the measures the government
chooses to counter the coronavirus. All in all, are you in favor of:
</td>

</td>

</table>
<table class=" lightable-classic-2" style='font-size: 13px; font-family: "Arial Narrow", "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; width: auto !important; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;'>
<thead>
<tr>
<th style="text-align:right;">
Response Code
</th>
<th style="text-align:left;">
Response Label
</th>
<th style="text-align:left;">
Response Wording
</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>

<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
1
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Much stricter measures to combat the virus (curfew, area ban).
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Veel strengere maatregelen om het virus tegen te gaan (avondklok,
gebiedsverbod).
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
2

</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
3
</td>

The measures chosen by the government.
</td>

</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
4
</td>

</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">

afgeschermd worden.
</td>
</tr>

5
</td>

immediately.

<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">

onmiddellijk op gang te brengen.

<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
It is easier in the Netherlands for a man to become a minister than for
a woman.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Het is in Nederland voor een man makkelijker om minister te worden dan
voor een vrouw.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
4
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Political parties must do more to ensure that the number of women in the
House of Representatives increases.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Politieke partijen moeten meer doen om te zorgen dat het aantal vrouwen
in de Tweede Kamer toeneemt.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
5
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Women have fewer opportunities in politics in the Netherlands than men.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Vrouwen krijgen in Nederland minder kansen in de politiek dan mannen.
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

### Block I: News Consumption

<table class=" lightable-classic-2 table" style='font-size: 13px; font-family: "Arial Narrow", "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; width: auto !important; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;'>

<td style="text-align:left;width: 15em; ">
Label
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 65em; ">
newscons\_freq

</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 15em; ">
Question wording ENG
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 65em; ">
How many days in the past two weeks have you followed the following
sources to learn something about politics and current affairs?
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 15em; ">
Question wording NL
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 65em; ">
Hoeveel dagen in de afgelopen twee weken heeft u de volgende bronnen
gevolgd om iets te weten te komen over politiek en actualiteiten?
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>

### Block C: Issue Association

<table class=" lightable-classic-2 table" style='font-size: 13px; font-family: "Arial Narrow", "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; width: auto !important; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;'>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 15em; ">
Question wording ENG
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 65em; ">
Political parties take positions on various subjects. We ask you what
subject you think of each party’s views below. Which subject comes to
mind first at \[party & party leader\]?
</td>
</tr>
<tr>

Question wording NL
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 65em; ">
Politieke partijen nemen over verschillende onderwerpen standpunten in.
We vragen u aan welk onderwerp u bij de standpunten van elke partij
hieronder denkt. Welk onderwerp komt als eerste bij u op bij \[partij &
partijleider\]?
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

### Block E: Political Background

<table class=" lightable-classic-2 table" style='font-size: 13px; font-family: "Arial Narrow", "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; width: auto !important; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;'>

Label
</td>

rile\_self

<td style="text-align:left;width: 15em; ">
Question wording ENG
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 65em; ">
In politics there is often talk about left and right. Where would you
put yourself on this scale?
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:left;width: 15em; ">
Question wording NL

In de politiek wordt vaak gesproken over links en rechts. Waar zou u
uzelf op deze schaal plaatsen?
</td>

### Block F: Trust

<table class=" lightable-classic-2 table" style='font-size: 13px; font-family: "Arial Narrow", "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; width: auto !important; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;'>

</td>

</td>

</td>

2

3

4

<table class=" lightable-classic-2 table" style='font-size: 13px; font-family: "Arial Narrow", "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; width: auto !important; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;'>
<thead>
<tr>
<th style="text-align:right;position: sticky; top:0; background-color: #FFFFFF;">
F1\_suffix
</th>
<th style="text-align:left;position: sticky; top:0; background-color: #FFFFFF;">
Statements ENG
</th>
<th style="text-align:left;position: sticky; top:0; background-color: #FFFFFF;">
Statements NL
</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
1
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Politicians don’t care about the opinions of people like me.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Politici maken zich niet druk om de mening van mensen zoals ik.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
2
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
The political parties are only interested in my vote and not in my
opinion.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
De politieke partijen zijn alleen maar geïnteresseerd in mijn stem en
niet in mijn mening.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
3
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Against their better judgment, politicians promise more than they can
deliver.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Tegen beter weten in beloven politici meer dan ze kunnen waarmaken.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
4
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
You become a member of parliament more by your political friends than by
your skills.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Kamerlid word je eerder door je politieke vrienden dan door je
bekwaamheden.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
5
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Most politicians are skilled people who know what they are doing.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
De meeste politici zijn bekwame mensen die weten wat ze doen.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
6
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Politicians are able to solve the most important problems.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Politici zijn in staat om de belangrijkste problemen op te lossen.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
7
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
I feel well represented by Dutch politicians.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Ik voel mij goed vertegenwoordigd door Nederlandse politici.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
8
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
What in politics is called ‘making compromises’ is actually just
betraying your principles.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Wat men in de politiek ‘het sluiten van compromissen’ noemt, is
eigenlijk gewoon het verraden van je principes.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
9
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
A strong head of government is good for the Netherlands, even if he
stretches the rules a bit to get things done.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
Een sterke regeringsleider is goed voor Nederland, ook als deze de
regels wat oprekt om dingen voor elkaar te krijgen.
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:right;width: 15em; ">
10
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
The most important political decisions should be made by the people and
not by politicians.
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 60em; ">
De belangrijkste politieke beslissingen moeten worden genomen door het
volk en niet door politici.
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<table class=" lightable-classic-2 table" style='font-size: 13px; font-family: "Arial Narrow", "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif; width: auto !important; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;'>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 15em; ">
Question wording ENG
</td>
<td style="text-align:left;width: 65em; ">
You will now be shown 6 statements that have to do with Dutch party
leaders. We would like to know from you to what extent the statement
applies to the party leader. Below you can indicate whether a party
leader is unknown to you.
</td>

Question wording NL

U krijgt nu 6 stellingen te zien die te maken hebben met de Nederlandse
partijleiders. Wij willen graag van u weten in hoeverre de uitspraak van
toepassing is op de partijleider. Hieronder kunt u aangeven of een
partijleider onbekend is bij u.
